        <div class="container2">  <!-- RULES + ASKBOX -->
            <div id="cont">
            
            <div class="guidebox">
                <h1>Guidelines</h1>
                
                <ul>
                    <li>Please have a clear understanding that the <strong>mun does not equal the muse</strong>. I cannot stress this enough. I do not harbor the same thoughts as my muses and my creative writing does not justify what they may do or say.</li>
                    <li>Be Kind and Understanding as I'm still fairly new to Tumblr roleplay.</li>
                    <li>No Godmodding under any circumstance although should you question yourself, feel free to IM me.</li>
                    <li>I am OC friendly although I do have the right to decline should the connection be lacking.</li>
                    <li>Do not pressure me for replies, as it likely will kill my motivation to even consider it. If you really want a reply from me, be patient, that's how you'll get it. I'd say give me about a <strong>week</strong> before giving me a friendly reminder if you haven't seen a reply.</li>
                    <li>I do not roleplay with <strong>Personal Blogs</strong>.</li>
                    <li>I only roleplay with mutuals, however anyone is free to send in asks.</li>
                    <li>My only <strong>trigger</strong> happens to be <em><strong>drug talk</strong></em> of any sort, in which case please tag it so I can avoid seeing it. Otherwise, feel free to do as you please. Should you have any triggers of your own, please alert me so that I may tag them accordingly.</li>
                    <li>This blog will interact with any and all canon characters, be they problematic or not. If you have a problem with that, plan accordingly.</li>
                    <li>Anon Hate/Negativity will be deleted on sight. Don't waste my time with it.</li>
                    <li>If you don't wish to see certain muses or ships, feel free to <strong><em>blacklist</em></strong> those tags. I tag every muse and ship and you're welcome to avoid them if you'd rather not clutter your dash. You can find the full tag list <a href="http://galaxythixf.tumblr.com/Tags">HERE</a>.</li>
                </ul>
                    
                <ul>
                    <li>I will actively avoid drama and call out posts, as I'm not interested in sinking into negativity. If you happen to do this often, you will most likely be unfollowed. I am simply here to have fun and I'm not interested in any drama.</li>
                </ul>
                    
                <h2>Regarding The Muse List</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>If A Muse is listed as "Unavailable" It simply means that I'm working on those icons. Usually it doesn't last long before they become available again. Give or take a day or so. I've made a FAQ list to keep my rules from appearing cluttered, listed <a href="http://galaxythixf.tumblr.com/FAQ">HERE</a>. </li></ul>
                    
                <h2>Regarding Writing</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>I am capable of writing Para/Novella although depending on the thread I may also do One Liners.</li></ul>
                
                <h2>Regarding NSFW/Smut</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>I will not be writing any smut on this blog, simply because it makes me uncomfortable. This is my personal preference but <em>you</em> can do whatever you want.</li>
                    <li>However, dirty jokes will still appear - as some of my muses are foul mouthed.</li>
                </ul>
                
                <h2>Regarding Sensitivity</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>I tend to favor writing particularly <strong>dark scenes</strong> but I will tag them accordingly. That being said, that will not be the only thing written on this blog. I assure you, there will most likely be <em>fluff</em> as well as <em>crack</em> on here.</li></ul>
                    
                <h2>Regarding Crossovers</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>Out of everything, I believe this is where I'll be the pickiest. I will accept certain characters over others if I feel either a connection with the mun or a particularly grand idea for interactions. Should the chemistry be right, I will most likely accept.</li></ul>
                    
                <h2>In Conclusion?</h2>
                <ul>
                    <li>I do enjoy getting to know my roleplaying partner. The joy of roleplaying is not only having interesting interactions with the muses but with the muns as well. Feel free to IM me should you have an idea you'd like to try or perhaps a meme or post regarding our muses. The connection between muns is what keeps roleplaying alive and I certainly value that.</li>
                    <li>Lastly, let's have some <em><strong>fun!</strong></em></li></ul>
                
                <!-- for credits you can look up 'CREDIT POP UP' and put all the credits for icons, psds, artwork etc there -->

        <div class="about-box">
        <h4>About</h4>
        
        <table>
        <!-- Fill in the basics of your muse here. Feel free to remove or edit to your hearts content! -->

    <hr>
    <h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ CLASS A THINKS IT'S SO GREAT. WELL, LET'S SHOW 'EM... WHY WE IN CLASS B HUNG BACK AND PLACED LOW IN THE PRELIMINARIES ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Neito is a young man of average height with slick blond hair, which gets shorter the further down his head it goes, styled so that it’s parted to the right, his bangs left hanging over his right eye. His irises are a periwinkle blue, his pupils white and his eyes are shaped so that they’re slanting downwards towards the far sides of his face, usually left half-closed, this, along with his signature smirk and head tilt, giving him a rather contemptuous look. The girls admit in the Light Novels that Monoma has a handsome face, but it’s ruined by his personality." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Neito_Monoma">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Neito is shown to be calm, collected, and intelligent. Among Class 1-B's students, he's the most fervent about wanting to topple Class 1-A's popularity. He is also disagreeable, sarcastic, and vocal. He seems to be jealous of Class 1-A's popularity, but also worries that the fact that they are always getting into trouble will get the rest of the school in trouble too. When he hears that Class 1-A fails in some way, he will usually laugh out loud and passive-aggressively ask how it's possible for them to fail since they are meant to be the superior class." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Neito_Monoma">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>
    
    <swoop> <!-- ABOUT / BACKSTORY -->
        
        <h4>Backstory</h4>
        <div class="about-box"><p>
        
        Backstory here! ♡
        
        </p></div>
        
        <h4>Family</h4>
        <div class="about-box"><p>
        <b>Monoma Keio:</b><br>
        Quirk: Duplicate - He's able to create copies of anything non-living via touch. Each copy is connected to him—almost like an extension of his body. Meaning no matter the location of the copied material, he'd essentially be able to track its location.<p>

He's a bit of an odd man, as most describe him. His expressions often look a bit smug or disingenuous but whether or not that's true is usually up for debate. He's quite the silver tongue and enjoys making light conversation to ease the worries of his patients or any suspecting individuals so for the most part he seems to just have an unfortunate resting face. Deep down however, he's fond of being manipulative to gain the upper hand. Usually rather relaxed and composed. Met his wife in college and the two have an entertaining back and forth dynamic that seems to work out.<p>

Despite his legitimate personality, he's well known for being an excellent doctor.<p>

        <hr>
        <b>Monoma Naho:</b><br>
        <b>Quirk:</b> Mimicry - She's able to mimic a person's voice with total accuracy for five minutes. The voices she's able to mimic can be anyone she's heard before.
        
        <hr>
        <b>Monoma Minori:</b><br>
        <b>Quirk:</b> Mimicry - She's able to mimic a person's voice with total accuracy for five minutes. The voices she's able to mimic can be anyone she's heard before.<p>

She's the eldest of the three children. Minori doesn't remember much before Neito was born but she did like to baby him before he could speak. As Neito got older the two of them bickered and fought far more often. Their disputes were usually put to rest after their father or a nanny's intervention ... usually. Once Kioshi was born their fighting seemed to dull down, mostly because they had no choice when left to take care of their youngest brother.<p>

Unlike Neito, Minori's always had her eyes set on starting her own clothing line. She'll leave the hero work to her brother. Despite how much they argue, she still supports him and asks for Neito's opinion on certain designs if she needs it. She's pretty picky when it comes to designs.<p>

        <b>Dislikes:</b> Neito sometimes, pets<p>
        
        <b>Likes:</b> Clothes, Skating, Cooking
        
        <hr>
        <b>Monoma Kioshi</b><br>
        <b>Quirk:</b> Mime - Like a mime, he's able to create objects from his imagination and make them tangible for five minutes. Only one item at a time and despite bringing the object into reality, only Kioshi can see it. Others can feel, smell, hear or touch it, it just isn't visible.<p>
        
        He is the youngest of the three children. Kioshi is only five at the start of Neito's first year at UA. At home, he's a troublemaker that likes to get his hands on just about anything and causes a lot of trouble for the nanny. He likes to play hide and seek and climb on various places he shouldn't be. Around strangers he's very shy and prefers not to speak. He'll stare, point and play but refuse to speak. Sometimes he'll even bite them. Even after he's more comfortable with someone he still may not speak to them for unknown reasons.<p>
        
        As he gets older, his speech is still limited to family and incredibly close friends. He's grown to like playing with animals (although he's usually too rough with them) or stuffy his mouth full of sweets.<p>
        
        He's known to bite and toy with his brother but on some days he does cooperate and genuinely enjoy playing with Neito whenever he complies. He's relatively docile with Minori and Neito envies this.<p>
        
        <b>Dislikes:</b> Veggies, haircuts, naps, being picked up<p>
        
        <b>Likes:</b> Candy, animals, his hair, ducks
        
        </p></div>
    </swoop>

Katsuki is very intelligent and extremely perceptive, capable of strategic planning and holding some of the highest grades in his class, to the point that some even consider him a natural genius." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Katsuki_Bakugo">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'M NOT GONNA BE YOUR WORTHLESS PUNCHING BAG DEKU FOREVER....KACCHAN. I'M....I'M THE DEKU WHO ALWAYS DOES HIS BEST! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            <img src="https://media.tenor.com/images/7ffe215568ce01bc703e4cbaf1a7483c/tenor.gif"/>
            
            "Izuku is somewhat short for his age, his round face framed by a short mess of fluffy dark-green hair which sticks up at odd angles around his head, casting noticeably dark shadows onto itself. His eyes are large and somewhat circular, their irises the same green color as his hair, which at times are very watery, and are usually stretched quite wide, giving him an innocent, energized appearance. He has a set of four symmetrical freckles in diamond formations, one on each cheek, but despite these prominent traits, he's often described by others as being <br>
            plain-looking." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Izuku_Midoriya">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Izuku is also very diligent and strong-willed. His dream of becoming a Hero drove him to develop a habit of writing down notes about everything he knows in regards to their Quirks. Because of this practice, Izuku has developed a great analytical mind and is easily able to form complex battle plans in a matter of seconds, taking advantage of his allies' and enemies’ Quirks to put them in motion. Izuku externalizes his observations through endless mumbling, a habit which annoys or scares his peers. Izuku often writes down his observations in a notebook he refers to as Hero Analysis for the Future." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Izuku_Midoriya">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Tsuyu is a short girl of a relatively slender build compared to her classmates and has notably large hands. Her appearance is rather frog-like; she has a very wide mouth, which dips down a little in the middle just like that of a common frog, and oval-shaped eyes with large, black irises, their lower eyelashes visibly pronounced, and she also demonstrates some frog-like mannerisms, such as hopping on all fours instead of running and holding herself in a way that is somewhat connotative of a frog." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Tsuyu_Asui">[Source]</a>

Tsuyu prefers to be called "Tsu", but only by people she views as friends. She commonly refers to everyone with the honorific "-chan", save for teachers and other authority figures." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Tsuyu_Asui">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ WE'VE GOT TO START AT THE BOTTOM AND WORK UP! AND IF WE DON'T EARNESTLY CHEER EACH OTHER ON... WE'LL NEVER BE TOP HEROES! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Momo is a tall teenage girl with a rather mature physique. Her Quirk’s need for fat cells requires her to keep a fuller figure than her classmates. She has long black hair that is normally tied into a spiky ponytail with a large strand hanging on the right side of her face. Her eyes are thin and sharp, dark in color and paired with short eyebrows set in a determined expression." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Momo_Yaoyorozu">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Momo is a very prudent, dedicated person who acts as a natural leader. She is generally level-headed and calm in dangerous situations, but she isn't above falling into a panic. Momo can be blunt with her comments about people's mistakes and miscalculations, tending to be very honest and wishing to help her peers improve enough to become great heroes, like tutoring them on her home. Momo shows further development as a selfless hero who gets inspiration from others, realizing the important thing is to focus on saving her and help them out at that moment even if it means losing her provisional hero license. She displays excitement towards pass time with her friends or help them, Momo becomes upbeat and eager. She also tends to accidentally reveal how rich she is, yet most people understand she doesn't do it out of malice." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Momo_Yaoyorozu">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ HE'S GOING AFTER ME...! I'M HIS NATURAL PREY! YOU WOULD THINK THAT, CLASS A. THIS PSYCHOLOGICAL TRAP WAS SET... BEFORE THE MATCH EVEN BEGAN! THIS'S HOW I WORK. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Shihai is a tall young man with fluffy white hair and black eyes, which are long and thin in shape. His most prominent feature is his pitch black skin, its unusual color most likely due to the Quirk he possesses, and his face usually holds an unsure or irritated expression." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Shihai_Kuroiro">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            ""Shihai is a sly, deceitful schemer, who prefers to catch people off guard. Shihai, very much like Fumikage Tokoyami, appears to enjoy dark concepts and has a penchant for dramatic speech." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Shihai_Kuroiro">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

        <h4>Backstory</h4>
        <div class="about-box"><p>
        
        Backstory here! ♡
        
        </p></div>
        
        <h4>Family</h4>
        <div class="about-box"><p>
        
        <b>Kuroiro Higura:</b> <br>
        Quirk: Shadow Beast- A mutation Quirk that makes him look like a shadow with glowing white eyes. The rest of him is pitch black, akin to an actual shadow.<p>
        
        He's a school teacher of middle school students who takes his job very seriously. Although occasionally enjoys giving his students a good scare which he believes is healthy every once in a while. He's insistent that his sons also take part in this in order to make them bolder. Met his wife in school, high school sweethearts.<p>
        
        <b>Dislikes:</b> Sunlight, Messes <br>
        
        <b>Likes:</b> The Dark, Cartoons, His Job, His Family
        
        <hr>
        
        <b>Kuroiro Ria: </b> <br>
        <b>Quirk:</b> Hide and Seek - A teleportation ability called Hide and Seek. By touching a flat surface, like a wall or the ground, and drawing symbols in a circle, she can set and open a portal leading to an artificial shadow pocket. She's able to make three pockets at a time and each room is separate from the other. Since this requires her to be able to see in the dark, she has night vision and often squints throughout the day.<p>
        
        Reserved and observant. Enjoys writing her own novels and taunting her husband with childish scares. Seems to have a short fuse when things don't align with her own methods and tends to stray from the 'norm'. Spoils her sons whenever she's able to and often babies Shihai even after he's grown. She's a nurse at the local hospital but really has a passion for writing.<p>
        
        <b>Dislikes:</b> Bright lights<br>
        
        <b>Likes:</b> The Dark, Writing, Her Family
        
        <hr>
        
        <b>Kuroiro Genta:</b><br>
        <b>Quirk:</b> Shadow Suit - He's able to wrap his own shadow around himself to use a shield for his entire body. The appearance is eerily similar to his father, just smaller. This is less effective during the day, as it tends to flicker, if it even works at all. Since this requires him to be able to see in the dark, he has night vision and often squints throughout the day. During the night, the suit is more reliable and is even capable of expanding within a small radius to cause a small blackout around him.<p>
    
        He's incredibly sluggish and paranoid. Due to his "insomnia" he hardly ever gets enough sleep and tends to nod off sometimes. If not, he does tend to run off into creepy tangents at times without realizing. Sometimes quoting his own poetry. An aspiring Mangaka that takes pride in writing gruesome love stories. He's hardworking but a little messy and jumpy. He loathes his family's fascination with cheap scares and even more so when he's the target. Despite this however, he has a good relationship with his little brother, Shihai and sometimes sends him doodles while he's away at school.<p>
        
        <b>Dislikes:</b> Being scared, Bright Lights<br>
        
        <b>Likes:</b> Sleep, Poetry
        
        </p></div>

He doesn’t appear to have any notable eyebrows, and, like Eijiro Kirishima, he has rows of sharp, pointed teeth." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Tetsutetsu_Tetsutetsu">[Source]</a>

He tends to be very vocal about his intentions and has a one-track mind, often looking for the simplest solution to problems in order to solve them in the most direct manner. During battles, Tetsutetsu's direct personality shows through his tenacious and upfront fighting style. Determined to prove himself, Tetsutetsu desires to be put on the same skill level as the students of Class 1-A. Tetsutetsu appears to care deeply about his peers. He didn't attack the villains before ensuring Ibara Shiozaki's safety and didn't hesitate to throw himself in front of a bullet for Itsuka Kendo." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Tetsutetsu_Tetsutetsu">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I WAS WRONG. EVER SINCE COMING HERE... AND PRACTICALLY DYING... I FINALLY GET IT! BEING A HERO DOESN'T MAKE YOU COOL... THEY'RE HEROES BECAUSE THEY'RE COOL! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Minoru is a very short teenage boy with a large, round head, and rather puffy cheeks. His nose is small, stubby and points slightly upwards, and he has an unusually distinguishable philtrum, oval-shaped eyes with large, black pupils, and notably thin eyebrows. He has a head of very short dark purple hair with four large ball-shaped clumps resembling a mohawk." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Minoru_Mineta">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Minoru is timid, but perverted to the point of infamy, which makes him unpopular with the girls and even some of the boys, who consider his interests and mannerisms depraved. Minoru can be very hypocritical, criticizing others for perceived perverted behavior, even if they turn out to be nothing more than misunderstandings. Minoru is also one who always speaks his mind, even when it comes off as harsh and insulting due to his comments being more on the cynical side.Minoru easily freaks out in moments of great stress or fear, acting in an impulsive way, crying when the situation does not look favorable and abusing his Quirk recklessly, to the point of hurting himself in the process. Minoru is not a very confident fighter and may attempt to flee in highly disadvantageous situations. Minoru is shown to be surprisingly intelligent, able to score very high on tests, and being in the top half of Class 1-A's grades, despite being considered a slacker by the majority of the class. Additionally, he is quite capable of coming up with creative and competent strategies in order to achieve victory, pushing through his own flaws when the need arises." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Minoru_Mineta">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'VE HATED THIS SCHOOL CREDO FOR AS LONG AS I CAN REMEMBER! PLUS ULTRA; PROMINENCE BURN! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Enji is a tall, sturdily-built man with a very muscular physique. He has short crimson hair which he wears spiked up around his head and sharp turquoise eyes. His beard and mustache appear to be made of fire, but when he voluntarily turns off the flames on his face a small amount stubble shows around his jaw." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Enji_Todoroki">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Enji has been described by his son as a prideful and ambitious man driven by his goal to surpass All Might. His desire to surpass the number one hero has driven him in family matters too, having "created" (via quirk marriage) his children in hopes of having an offspring that could surpass All Might." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Enji_Todoroki">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ IF YOU'RE TRASH, AT LEAST BURN AND BE KINDLING FOR MY FLAMES ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Dabi is a fairly tall, pale young man of a slim, somewhat-lanky build, described to be in his early twenties. He has white hair with a few red streaks at its crown that spikes upward around his head, hanging low over his eyes, which are thin, turquoise in color, and heavily lidded. Before the reveal of his true identity, his hair was dyed black.<p>

His most striking features are undoubtedly the patches of gnarled, wrinkled, purple skin that cover much of his lower face and neck, all the way down past his collarbone, below his eyes, around his torso, and on his arms and legs due to his fire Quirk falling out of control at a young age and engulfing him in flames. These appear to be attached to the rest of his skin by multiple, crude surgical staples or hoop piercings." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Dabi">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Dabi is a stoic, aloof, confident, and focused individual who rarely shows emotion. He is intolerant of most people and can be very decisive. Dabi insulted Tomura immediately after meeting him and constantly does the same to his allies and his enemies. He was reluctant to introduce himself and rudely brushed off Tomura's inquiry about his true name." <a href="https://myheroacademia.fandom.com/wiki/Dabi">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>

He tends to show his excitement for a big challenge. However, Akihiko is a kind young man who will go out of his way to help someone." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Akihiko_Sanada">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ LIAR. YOU SAID YOU'D BELIEVE ME! I CAN'T TRUST ANY ADULTS. SO I'LL FIND HIM MYSELF. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Ken has styled short brown hair and eyes. Even as an elementary student, he is short for his age. At school and Tartarus, he wears a school uniform of Gekkoukan Elementary, with an orange jacket under his Gekkoukan jacket, and tennis shoes with white socks. On weekends off, he is seen wearing a long orange turtleneck sweater shirt with light orange sleeves and tan shorts. On the summer days off, he wears a black turtleneck shirt underneath his orange and black jersey (with an "8" on the back, referencing his Arcana) and black shorts." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Ken_Amada">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Despite his young age, Ken is very intelligent and mature. It is shown that this is a coping mechanism due to the death of his mother at a young age, which more-or-less forced him to give up his childhood. Besides being mature, Ken also knows several words that boys his age don't usually know, such as "bastard". He is very polite to others, and never misses a chance to show respect where respect is due. He is also honest, diligent, and deeply caring towards his peers, particularly the members of SEES. Ken is shown to like and care a great deal for animals, such as Koromaru." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Ken_Amada">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ YOU DON'T KNOW SHIT ABOUT HOW I FEEL! YUKIKO MIGHT DIE FROM THIS, FOR CRYING OUT LOUD! I'M GOING, AND THAT'S THAT! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Chie has dyed light brown bowl-shaped hair and brown eyes. As with most playable characters in the game, Chie wears a modified Yasogami High uniform with a light green, high collared athletic jacket adorned with several decorative pins (including a smiley face) and underneath her mini skirt she wears short black compression shorts. In summer, however, she is seen wearing the school's standard summer uniform, having wrapped her jacket around her hips." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Chie_Satonaka">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Chie is energetic and outgoing, the "extrovert" compared to Yukiko being the "introvert." She has a bright and upbeat personality, often trying to cheer up the group by joking about the case. She can be somewhat short tempered, especially with Yosuke, and is slow to back down from a challenge. Chie has strong sense of justice and a fierce desire to protect others. She is known to defend classmates, children, and strangers from being threatened and attacked by local delinquents. Even when outnumbered, she does not hesitate to intervene and speak out. Though reckless in putting herself into dangerous situations, she is willing to sacrifice herself for the sake of others." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Chie_Satonaka">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ AS LONG AS YOU TAKE ME LIGHTLY DUE TO MY SIZE, YOU WILL NEVER DEFEAT ME. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Naoto is the shortest member of the Investigation Team. She is androgynous in appearance with short blue hair and gray eyes (blue in The Animation and Arena). She wears Yasogami High's gakuran, with the exception of one optional occasion in which she wears a seifuku-style school uniform. Naoto is often seen wearing formal clothing such as blue shirts, ties and her trademark blue cap. On days off during winter, she wears a dark blue double-breasted cardigan coat (which she says is custom made) with a light blue bowtie (on her white dress shirt underneath) and yellow buttons and plaid blue pants. Naoto's summer outfit, however, is reminiscent of the clothing of Kyouji Kuzunoha and consists of a light blue shirt and a yellow necktie." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Naoto_Shirogane">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Having lost both her parents in a car accident when she was very young, Naoto is an orphan who acts very mature in spite of her age. As a descendant of a respected lineage of famous detectives, she wears formal clothing and deepens her voice when she speaks in a sophisticated, stilted manner. She is generally very serious, focused and mission-oriented. She rarely jokes around which can make her seem like a killjoy or party pooper when the team is involved in silly antics. In Persona 4 Arena, Kanji calls her out on this, saying she is too "uptight" and it makes her seem distant and on a different wavelength. One of Naoto's insecurities is her lack of friends; she has difficulty making friends and is lonely as a result." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Naoto_Shirogane">[Source]</a>

They're comfortable with any pronouns being used for them. They/Them, She/Her, or He/Him. It makes no difference to them. For this reason I tend to use whichever depeneding on what my partner uses first. If not, I'll pick for myself. If you have a preference please let me know!
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ RISKING OUR LIVES TO STOP ROTTEN ADULTS... THAT'S WHY WE'RE PHANTOM THIEVES! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Futaba is a young girl with hip-length black hair dyed bright orange, with straight-cut bangs and two long strands in the front along with a single small, thin strand at the top. Her brown eyes also seem to have some faint purple tones in them, appearing mauve. She wears large black circular glasses, and is almost always seen wearing a set of AKG K845BT headphones with red ear cushions. She seems to be very short, even compared to other girls." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Futaba_Sakura">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "With a case of social anxiety bordering on agoraphobia, combined with the trauma of losing her mother Wakaba Isshiki, Futaba is strongly discomfited by going outside. When the protagonist first meets her, she is a hikikomori who does not attend school and almost never leaves her room. She communicates with the world remotely via the Internet, and her adoptive father Sojiro Sakura enables her lifestyle out of guilt that he could not protect her from trauma. Having disconnected herself from humanity and the world beyond her apartment, Futaba is lonely, lives without passion and enthusiasm, suffers from suicidal depression, and questions the point in her living. Futaba begins to change after meeting the protagonist and the other Phantom Thieves, opening up to them more and becoming more relaxed around them. Once she's truly comfortable around others, she shows her childish side and likes teasing her friends." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Futaba_Sakura">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ WELL, BECAUSE I'M A PSYCHIC, OF COURSE. HAHA, I'M ONLY JOKING. IN TRUTH, I'M A ROOKIE DETECTIVE. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Akechi has shaggy, neck length brown hair with bangs and reddish-brown eyes. He wears a tan peacoat with black buttons, striped black and white tie, black pants, black gloves and black loafers. His casual winter outfit consists of a white long sleeve shirt with flaps under a blue diamond sweater vest, beige pants and brown shoes." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Goro_Akechi">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Behind his popularity he is quite lonely and yearns to be loved. He was abandoned by his father, subsequently lost his mother to suicide and never had close friends. He was passed around the foster care system as an orphan and has developed a far more jaded worldview than he initially lets on, even calling himself an unwanted child. He has a desperate desire to be acknowledged, which he is forthright about being the primary drive for his actions as a detective. He also has a narcissistic element to his personality, wishing for others to see him as a hero and those who oppose him as the villains. Akechi claims that he has carefully crafted his public image in the hopes that it would make people accept him. He has the public's support only if he upholds the pretense of being a charismatic idol detective." <a href="https://megamitensei.fandom.com/wiki/Goro_Akechi">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ MY GREATEST PLEASURE COMES WHEN SUCH PEOPLE CRUMPLE TO THEIR KNEES AND I LOOK DOWN UPON THEIR DISBELIEVING FACES AS THEIR PLANS FAIL.♥ ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Hisoka's appearance is similar to that of a magician or jester. He is tall and has light skin and a very muscular physique. His attire is usually adorned with various suit symbols (♦/♦ ♣/♣ ♥/♥ ♠/♠) on the front and back torso, and he changes outfits in each story arc. He wears face paint of a star (★) on his right cheek and a teardrop (💧) on his left cheek, and like his attire, in the 2011 anime, his face paint also occasionally changes colors. During the Greed Island arc, Hisoka wears the Greed Island Ring on his left middle finger. And in the 13th Hunter Chairman Election arc, Hisoka wears a pair of earrings with ornamental hearts. For unknown reasons, Hisoka has long, pointed nails, giving his hands a claw-like appearance, hinting at his sinister nature." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Hisoka_Morow">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Hisoka is portrayed as entirely self-serving, self-absorbed, and selfish; he does whatever he likes as long as it pleases him in some way. His insatiable love for spilling the blood of powerful fighters in combat and his enjoyment of extreme pain while doing so fuels his seemingly sadomasochistic desires. In order for them to grow to their full potential (so as to improve the pleasure of killing them later). Likewise, he grows excited to meet any new people he deems worthy of fighting or anyone with the potential to be a good fighter and entertain him in the future. The thrill of fighting strong Nen users in tactical battles and near-death experiences is an orgasmic experience for him. It is likely one of the reasons why he goes out of his way to find new toys to play with. If they break, he either loses interest or kills them before going out to find more potential prey." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Hisoka_Morow">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'M SO TIRED OF KILLING... I JUST WANT TO BE A KID. HANGING OUT, DOING STUFF WITH GON. THAT'S IT ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Killua has spiky silver hair, very pale skin, and blue eyes. His eyes change shape depending on the mood that he's in, narrowing and sharpening when he goes into assassination mode. Killua is fairly lean at the start of the series, due to constant physical conditioning and torture training he received when he was young. As time passes, he becomes more muscular and toned." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Killua_Zoldyck">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Initially, Killua is introduced as a character who appears similar to Gon: cheeky, cheerful, and full of mischievous ideas. However, contrasting Gon's politeness, Killua can be quite rude to others, mostly strangers and older people. He is most commonly known for having a sweet tooth; he loves everything sweet and spent almost 200 million Jenny Currency Symbol on snacks when he was at the Heavens Arena. His favorite snack is chocolate, specifically Chocolate Balls. He is also one of the quickest-thinking characters and often analyzes a situation with great ease and accuracy. In spite of his young age, his way of thinking, knowledge, and pragmatism give him the attitude of an adult. He is initially very confident about his own abilities. As time passed, Killua became humble about it; but when somebody compliments him, especially Gon, he becomes easily embarrassed." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Killua_Zoldyck">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>

            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Kurapika has medium blond hair with brown eyes; blue in the 1999 series (grey/dark grey in the 2011 series). His eyes glow a beautiful and coveted scarlet when experiencing intense emotion. In his first appearance in the series, he wears a blue tabard decorated with an orange-colored (red in the 2011 series) hem and a white full-body training suit underneath. He changes his tabard and training suit for the duration of the Yorknew City arc. His shoes are Chinese style winkle-picker flats." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Kurapika">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Kurapika is an intelligent individual, possessing vast knowledge. He is reticent; not one to open up to people easily and quite judgmental. His distance from others initially keeps him level-headed and moralistic, but his heart has been poisoned with sadness and hatred. Having been traumatized from losing everyone he loved at the age of twelve, Kurapika closes his heart to new people and remains introverted as to stay focused on his goal. Though Kurapika outwardly states that he desires to become a Blacklist Hunter and his ultimate goal is to capture the band of thieves that massacred his family, he is willing to compromise his personal morality and delve into the squalid side of society in order to achieve his goal. He is prone to fits of uncontrollable anger should the memory of his clan be insulted in any way. After becoming a professional Hunter, Kurapika starts upon a self-destructive path. His anger leads him to commit villainous acts of wrath as catharsis for his pain. Kurapika's reserved demeanor makes him very ruthless and unreasonable at times, but his friends are the only ones able to slightly settle his seething enough for him to think rationally. He slowly transitioned from considering his friendships to be a weakness hindering him from succeeding in his aims to appreciating their value." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Kurapika">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <div class="dropdown">

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">

He expressed a dislike for his Autopilot mode, not just because he cannot remember his actions in that mode, but also he cannot feel satisfaction for what he did while in autopilot In the manga, however, he was almost never shown not smiling, with notable exceptions of pouting when one of his "toys" (controlled victims) gets "broken" (dies), scowling when people handle electronics carelessly, and looked highly unsettled when walking in on Feitan reading a book by Trevor Brown next to a bloody corpse." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Shalnark">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ WELCOME, LADIES AND GENTLEMEN. LET US DO WITHOUT FORMAL GREETING... YOU ALL DIE NOW. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Feitan is short, lean, and muscular. He has black, mid-length hair, grey eyes, and a pale complexion. He wears dark, baggy clothes and a bandana sporting the trademark skull crest over his mouth. Feitan's spider tattoo has yet to be revealed." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Feitan_Portor">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Feitan is the Phantom Troupe's interrogator, being very proficient in the art of torture. His speech usually consists of few words and poor grammar; when angered, he speaks a language of unknown origin, different from the common language of the world. He is cold-natured but very loyal to Chrollo Lucilfer and the Phantom Troupe as a whole. He is implied to be deeply involved with all Phantom Troupe activities, remembering exact details of how long it's been since the last time all of the members have gathered together, what has changed since then and who the new members are or when Chrollo gave him instructions." <a href="https://hunterxhunter.fandom.com/wiki/Feitan_Portor">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'LL EAT IT! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Honey possesses a babyish face and is extremely short in height; his actual height being 148 cm (4'10"). His hair is short and honey-blond in color. When not in Ouran's school uniform, he tends to dress simply in the anime but outrageously in the manga. He is typically seen with his cousin Mori or his stuffed bunny Usa-Chan (a.k.a. Bun-Bun) by his side, and whenever he speaks, flowers float around his head; the only exceptions being when he is angry, upset or confused." <a href="https://ouran.fandom.com/wiki/Mitsukuni_%22Honey%22_Haninozuka">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Although he often appears dimwitted, Honey is actually highly intelligent and clever. Despite his generally positive nature, he angers easily when awakened from slumber and since his bloodtype is AB, most of the hosts believe that he has a split personality." <a href="https://ouran.fandom.com/wiki/Mitsukuni_%22Honey%22_Haninozuka">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ MEMORIES ARE MERELY INFORMATION. CREATING OR ERASING THEM IS NOT DIFFICULT. WHAT I WANT TO UNDERSTAND...IS THE "EMOTION" THAT REACHES BEYOND THEM. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Gowther has amber eyes and dark red hair (sometimes depicted as magenta) that reaches just past his jaw. His usual attire consists of a white shirt with gray long sleeves over a black cropped tank top as well as a pair of dark pants and short grey boots. After Bartra made him dress like a maid, Gowther adopted an unusual habit of wearing women's clothes." <a href="https://nanatsu-no-taizai.fandom.com/wiki/Gowther">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Gowther first shows himself speaking in his distinctive, emotionless manner. His expression never changes, being completely blank, and his speech bubbles are uniquely square, compared to the round bubbles of everyone else. Yet despite his emotionless nature, Gowther does care about others."<p>

"He is shown to be completely unaware of others' feelings, has shown an inability to understand the meaning of friendship. He often states things factually without realizing that what he says can upset people. Gowther decides to assist Elizabeth on her journey, not because of a desire for justice, but because he felt obligated as a member of the Seven Deadly Sins. Since Gowther doesn't understand emotions he goes to great lengths to understand them better."<p>

"He is shown to be completely unaware of others' feelings, has shown an inability to understand the meaning of friendship. He often states things factually without realizing that what he says can upset people." <a href="https://nanatsu-no-taizai.fandom.com/wiki/Gowther">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

            <td>    Harlequin "King" </td></tr>

        <tr><th>Birthday:</th>      
            <td>    April 1st </td></tr>
            
        <tr><th>Gender:</th>      
            <td>    Male (he/him) </td></tr>
            
        <tr><th>Race:</th>      
            <td>    Fairy </td></tr>

        <tr><th>Preference:</th>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'M THE FAIRY KING, SO I WANT TO PROTECT THE FOREST, MY PEOPLE, DIANE, EVERYTHING! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "King's fairy form resembles a young boy with short brown hair, a high forehead, thin eyebrows, and brownish-orange eyes. He wears a long orange and an aqua sweatshirt with a hood and navy blue sleeves, quarter-length navy blue pants, and short boots with large buttons matching his hoodie. He also carries a green leopard pattern pillow which is actually a transformation of his spear Chastiefol. Despite being a fairy, he has yet to grow visible wings.<p>

In his human form, he looks almost exactly like his wanted poster; large, fat and more ragged, perhaps hinting at how humans look to fairies. He wears an enlarged version of the clothes he wears as a fairy, though he can freely change the clothes he wears in this form." <a href="https://nanatsu-no-taizai.fandom.com/wiki/King">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "In his first appearance, he is shown to be an ally to the Holy Knights and is willing to wipe out anyone who gets in his way along with the person he is after. Meliodas once referred him as the Sins' "pet" when describing King to Elizabeth; and indeed, King's slowness to resort to unnecessary harm may well make him as their most morally-upright member. He appeared to be somewhat lazy, preferring to levitate in most occasions. In the past, he was shown to be a compassionate character who returned stuffed animals stolen by Ban to children. Furthermore, it appears that he is an emotional person who cries easily. King has trouble admitting his affection for Diane. Although he enjoys being with Meliodas and Diane, he could not bring himself to express it. He cares deeply for his sister, Elaine."<p>

"King is also shown to have a caring side. He helps the Seven Deadly Sins in their battle against the Holy Knights, although he claims it is merely for Diane. Despite being the Sin of Sloth, he is hardworking and serious at times. When King joins the group, he starts to act like the only rational one in the group, and questions his teammates' erratic and slightly insane actions, such as their nonchalance about losing their sacred treasures. When forced to do something he dislikes, King can easily be motivated if it will make Diane happy. Despite King's kind personality, he is not against killing someone, if pushed to his limits."<p>

"Since he is the Sin of Sloth, he is shown as somewhat lazy, preferring to levitate in most occasions. In the past, he was shown to be a compassionate character." <a href="https://nanatsu-no-taizai.fandom.com/wiki/King">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ SOMEONE MUST PUT A STOP TO THIS CYCLE OF THE STRONG TRAMPLING THE WEAK. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            Illegally good looking

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Dimitri is a sincere young man who seems like the embodiment of chivalry, but a shade of darkness lies beneath his cheerful demeanor. Despite being a royal, he dislikes formality and prefers his allies to be frank. Dimitri enjoys combat training but dislikes fragile objects. He also became a capable dancer under Edelgard's tutelage. Dimitri suffers from ageusia and survivor's guilt as a result of the Tragedy of Duscur, this grief also causes him to be overcome with a berserker's fury or see apparitions of the dead." <a href="https://fireemblem.fandom.com/wiki/Dimitri">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ THERE'S NOTHING TO BE GAINED FROM FIGHTING SOMEONE NOT WORTH DUELING, AFTER ALL. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            Illegally good looking

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Presenting himself as a sharp-tongued lone wolf, Felix is so devoted to honing his swordsmanship that he will immediately challenge any strong person he meets to a duel. He expresses interest and respect in particularly strong swordsmenValuing hard work, he always seeks to train and hone his ability, and treats anybody who gets in the way of that with rudeness, being particularly disdainful of those that rely on their noble privilege or Crest. Felix holds a certain cynicism for Faerghus' values of chivalry and virtue, and thus has complicated relationships with the majority of Blue Lions, while also being a source of arguments with his father. It is stated by Rodrigue that this is a direct result of Glenn's death during the Tragedy of Duscur, though Felix states it is also a result on his father's insistence on fulfilling his duty to the late king which he found foolish since being grounded by the dead only leads to misery. He freely speaks his mind, no matter how rude he sounds, but ultimately means well despite his attempts to mask his feelings of concern for his allies. His words of advice are often hidden behind insults and barbs." <a href="https://fireemblem.fandom.com/wiki/Felix">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ WHAT'S WRONG? YOU LOOK SLEEPY. ARE YOU SLEEPY BY ANY CHANCE? WELL, I AM. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            Illegally good looking

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Hating constraints and loving his freedom, Linhardt does his best to avoid worries and problems, and indulges in lazing about. Contrary to what this may indicate at first, Linhardt is far from useless, as he offers precise observation and criticism to his classmates in several of his support conversations, but he is unwilling to utilize his skills in a practical manner. He has a genuine interest in Crests, and when he gets into his research he can forget to even eat or sleep. That, accompanied by his unparalleled intellect makes him one of the smartest students in his class. However, he often flutters from interests and is only able to focus on whatever fancies him in the moment. Additionally, he is so disinterested in anything else that he will fall asleep when the topic of discussion shifts away from his interests. Despite their personalities and hobbies being different, he gets along well with Caspar.﻿ He has a strong dislike of blood, so much so that upon his first kill, he will be shocked and horrified at his actions." <a href="https://fireemblem.fandom.com/wiki/Linhardt">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝  FIGHT AND GET STRONGER, HE SAYS... GUESS IT CAN'T HURT TO TRY. I SURE HOPE I DON'T GET IN THE WAY! GOSH, THAT WOULD BE JUST AWFUL.. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>

        </p></div><br>

            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Donnel is a typical village boy "from the sticks" and is unaccustomed to life outside of his village. Though he was hesitant to ever enter battle, Donnel musters enough courage to stand up for himself and eventually join Chrom's army. His speech is vastly different compared to the rest of the army, speaking with a southern-farmer accent. In the midst of the war, before the final attack on Grima." <a href="https://fireemblem.fandom.com/wiki/Donnel">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ IT’S QUITE CONCERNING TO HAVE BEEN BROUGHT HERE WITH THE LAUNDRY STILL OUT DRYING… ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Kai is described as having the beauty of a woman. He has a slender build, shoulder-length black hair parted down the middle, and dark eyes. Kai often has a blank, inexpressive face. He wears a red-orange apron given to him by the Chidouin family over a long-sleeved black changshan with orange trimming. Kai's usually seen holding various kitchen utensils behind his back, specifically a ladle, spatula, and frying pan. Like the other participants, he also has a collar around his neck." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Kai_Satou">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Kai has a seemingly aloof and absentminded nature. He's often quiet, even during intense discussions and accusations. Because of his quiet nature, he isn't considered to be much of a person of interest to the group. Though like the others, he makes it apparent that he wishes to try his best to contribute to their advancement, even if his withdrawn demeanor and weird aura put Sara off." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Kai_Satou">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Main

                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Crossover
    &emsp;&emsp;<b>Timeline:</b>    BNHA
    
                </div><p>
                <a class="vertag" href="/tagged/VERSE TAG">verse tag</a>
                <img class="verimg" src="https://via.placeholder.com/75"/>
                Kai is the youngest of an organized crime group by the name of Asu-naro. The son of a mid-ranked member of the organization. The group has long since been operating with secret affairs that involve kidnappings whose motives otherwise remain unknown. Raised as a brutal assassin he was assigned to infiltrate the school known as UA to prepare meals in order to transfer information back and forth. However, the more time he spends with the students and his coworkers the less inclined he is to cooperate with his own party.
       
       
       
       <br><br><br><br>
        </p>
            </ver>
            
            <ver>
                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Brothers in Crime
    &emsp;&emsp;<b>Timeline:</b>    AU
    
                </div><p>
                <a class="vertag" href="/tagged/VERSE TAG">verse tag</a>
                
                In this verse Kai's upbringing is relatively the same except he grows up along side his human, younger, half brother, Rio (Rio Ranger). The relationship between the two of them is strained due to the lack of communication and emotional vulnerability on both accounts but the future fortunately, looks bright.
       
        </p>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I WAS RIDING WITH MY PARTN… WELL, A COWORKER. BUT I ENDED UP ALONE FOR JUST A SECOND, GOT CONKED OUT, AND HERE WE ARE. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Keiji is a tall man with a muscular build. He has short, fluffy, bleached blonde hair and gray eyes with dark circles underneath. He wears a short-sleeved gray shirt with a black vest over it. And wears brown pants and black dress shoes." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Keiji_Shinogi">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Keiji is shown to be pretty casual and level-headed during the Death Game, though he comes off as shady to some of the participants. He usually refers to himself as "the friendly policeman" in an effort to establish himself as trustworthy and makes a pretense of being less cunning than he really is.<p>

He's observant and canny and is quite good at reading other people and knows when to speak up and when to leave them be. <p>

He's also encouraging and gentle with the younger participants, making it his job to at least keep watch over Gin." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Keiji_Shinogi">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

        <table>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I WAS ON THE WAY TO MY USUAL PART-TIME JOB AT A CONVENIENCE STORE. IT’S A BAD PART OF TOWN… AND I WAS AWARE OF HOW DANGEROUS IT COULD BE AT NIGHT… BUT THE NIGHT SHIFT WAGES ARE GOOD… SO. SUDDENLY, SOMEONE ATTACKED ME. I CAN’T REMEMBER WHAT ELSE HAPPENED THEN. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Sou is a young male described as frail. He stands with poor posture. He has fluffy, light teal hair with slightly darker teal eyes.<p>

Sou's outfit consists of a green beanie, a pale brown long-sleeved shirt tucked into khaki pants, and a purple jacket. His pants are held up with a brown belt with a gold buckle. Sou also wears a pink-orange polka-dotted scarf with tassels. The polka-dots are colored in a stripped, reflected pattern of peach, pink, and dark brown. He has also been shown to wear light brown fuzzy boots.<p>

Being a participant of the Death Game, he wears a collar device." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Shin_Tsukimi">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "At first introduction, Sou is generally friendly but a bit standoffish. He's secretive due to being distrustful of the other participants. Despite this, he helps everyone discover secrets about where they're trapped.

Sou is canny and intelligent, but due to his suspicious nature, has a habit of jumping to negative conclusions, especially in regards to Sara. He cannot comprehend Sara's charisma and is both resentful and envious of how she manages to gain the others' trust.

Survival is his main priority, and with knowledge of his survival rates (provided by the organization), his previous personality snaps and warps to what he believes would better serve his continued existence. This also means lying to achieve whatever ends, and skillfully at that.

He is a skilled computer hacker and appears to care for Kanna Kizuchi." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Shin_Tsukimi">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ WELL ... I DO WANNA KILL ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Sou has bright green hair and wide disconcerting, jade eyes. His hair is short and wavy with a rattail.

He stands slightly hunched over. His outfit consists of a black suit, red tie, and the same scarf that Shin Tsukimi wears.

The Sou Hiyori doll, Midori, wears a Floor Master collar. His body is, in fact, over 50% doll but still has human parts to it. His human hands are swapped with Mai's doll hands." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Sou_Hiyori">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Sou is familiar to most of the Death Game participants, including Keiji, Q-taro, Kanna, Alice, Reko, and Shin. However, none of them could clearly remember what relation they have with him. Even Alice, who had allegedly murdered him, and Reko, who had been deeply affected by the murder case, did not remember Sou's face until they were staring right at his picture." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Sou_Hiyori">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ QUOTE ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Ranmaru is a thin, short, teenage boy with gray-blue eyes and soft, fluffy-looking white hair with bangs. <p>

Ranmaru wears a high school gakuran uniform, with an especially cropped top. The pants are held up with a light gray belt. His body is wrapped in bandages from collarbone to the palms of his hands and he wears a shuriken-shaped pendent. He's also wearing indoor school slippers. <p>

He wears a collar as do all participants, dummies, and floor masters. Like all of the dummies, Ranmaru wears one that was specially made for doll usage." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Ranmaru_Kageyama">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Ranmaru is a casual and easy-going boy. He is generally placid in nature, although occasionally flustered, such as when Sara holds his hand. He seems to come off as nervous or awkward in certain situations. Ranmaru also tries to keep quiet and distant until provoked.

He is shown to be compassionate and expresses a want to be useful to the others." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Ranmaru_Kageyama">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ BEFORE I WAS BROUGHT HERE… I HAD RARE PLANS FOR A VISITATION. BUT WHEN I ENTERED THE VISITING ROOM, NO ONE CAME. BY THE TIME I STARTED TO FIND IT ODD, MY SENSES WERE ALREADY FADING ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Alice has a "gaudy hairstyle," as opined by Sara; separated into two parts; the right half is blue and covers his eye, and the left side is shaved close to his head and colored into magenta and yellow stripes. He wears a striped prison uniform that is frayed at the collar and sleeves, with handcuffs hanging from his left wrist. He also has a ball and chain wrapped around his waist.

In a childhood flashback, Alice is shown to have long blue hair that covers his right eye. He gowns a green striped sweater with a white popped-out collar and a pair of brown pants.

Being a participant in the Death Game, he also wears a collar device around his neck." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Alice_Yabusame">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Alice has a short fuse and is one of the few participants that has little trust for the rest of the group. Because of his attitude in that no one can be trusted, he tends to go off on his own and often pushes others away when they want to work or talk to him. He is quite aggressive in the way he speaks, but with enough persuasion and trust he can be kind and helpful.

His mother tried to raise him like he was a girl during his childhood. Because of this, he often speaks in a feminine manner." <a href="https://yourturntodie.fandom.com/wiki/Alice_Yabusame">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ I'VE PROTECTED IT. YOU TOLD ME... THIS IS MORE IMPORTANT TO YOU... THAN YOUR OWN LIFE. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Zenitsu is a young man with fair skin and downward-sloped, scared-looking eyes that fade from soft brown to gold. He has short, yellow hair of varying lengths, cutting off squarely at the ends where it fades to a darker orange color, that falls in front of his face in uneven bangs. Before he became a Demon Slayer, Zenitsu's hair was originally black, but it turned the color it is currently when he was struck by lightning during his training." <a href="https://kimetsu-no-yaiba.fandom.com/wiki/Zenitsu_Agatsuma">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Zenitsu is a coward; always claiming he doesn't have long to live due to the dangerous job of being a Demon Hunter. He also has rather low self-esteem despite his strength, to the point that he thinks he's actually useless. Zenitsu is in a constant state of fear and always cries and tries to run away at the sight of danger, claiming he wants to live a modest, normal life, instead of that of a Demon Slayer in which he just thinks he's useless all the time. However, despite these weaknesses, Zenitsu still wants to live up to the expectations others set up for him and will try his hardest when he is needed to. He holds great respect and admiration towards his comrades and his teacher. Zenitsu is also shown to be something of a wannabe womanizer; he tends to hit on girls who he thinks are cute and ask them to marry him, much to their annoyance." <a href="https://kimetsu-no-yaiba.fandom.com/wiki/Zenitsu_Agatsuma">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>

        <h4>About</h4>
        
        <table>
        <!-- Fill in the basics of your muse here. Feel free to remove or edit to your hearts content! -->
        
        <tr><th>Name:</th>      
            <td>    Katie Holt </td></tr>

        <tr><th>Birthday:</th>      
            <td>    April 3rd </td></tr>
            
        <tr><th>Gender:</th>      
            <td>    Female (she/her) </td></tr>

            <td>    Green </td></tr>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ YOU CAN'T KEEP ME OUT. I'LL FIND THE TRUTH, I'LL NEVER STOP!!! ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Pidge's a shorter-than-average human girl, and her appearance reflects her androgynous personal style. She's the slimmest and shortest of the Paladins. She has brown eyes, fair skin, and disheveled light brown hair. She makes no obvious effort to cut or style her hair, so it tends to form two spikes on either side of her head and unruly bangs. She dons wire-framed, round, circular glasses with fake lenses to address her lack of actual visual impairment. These were given to her by her brother Matt, who originally needed them before the Garrison fixed his eyesight. Matt gave them to Pidge before he left on the Kerberos Mission with their father, Sam, and Shiro. She has kept them with her ever since." <a href="https://voltron.fandom.com/wiki/Pidge_(Legendary_Defender)">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Pidge is a technical genius, and is more than capable of quickly learning how to operate advanced alien technology. She is also an intensely private person, often needing some measure of personal space and has a hard time bonding with others. She had a profoundly hard time with her psychic training due to this deep-seated aspect of her personality. Pidge is also something of a hoarder, collecting every last piece of new technology she can get her hands on, and trying to create something better out of even the most advanced machines available. She is always looking to improve upon what is around her, allowing her to adapt and thrive even in the most difficult or unconventional circumstances, even if it means dismantling alien tech and risking the lives of herself and those around her. She is very close to her brother, often having goofed around by hacking into their father's communication systems while he was on missions. Their resemblance is further noted due to their similarly scientific areas of perseverance, developed fierce personalities, and even their fighting styles pack the same wallop. Pidge also seems as close to her father as to her brother if not closer. When it comes to subjects about her family, Pidge can be single-minded and very stubborn to the point she will not listen to anyone and can be very irrational." <a href="https://voltron.fandom.com/wiki/Pidge_(Legendary_Defender)">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>

After his mother passed away two years ago, he's been in the custody of his Aunt Natsumi, Satomi's younger sister. He chooses not to live under the same roof, instead makes his own living by working part-time and living alone. He successfully keeps his fight matches for money a secret from his aunt. He remains undefeated in the Underground Match, a series of fight battles that his friend, Seiji Ananome, introduced due to his excellent physical abilities and fighting instincts. A senior at Shinza High School. Normally quiet and indifferent, he can be considerate of his friends and family. An infamous delinquent known for his fighting skill, his name's well known by others like him." <a href="https://death-mark.fandom.com/wiki/Akira_Kijima">[Source]</a>

    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
