    <swoop> <!-- ABOUT / VERSES -->
    
        <h4>Verses</h4>
        <div class="about-box">
        
            <ver>
                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Main    
    &emsp;&emsp;<b>Timeline:</b>    Canon  
                </div><p>
                <a class="vertag" href="/tagged/VERSE TAG">verse tag</a>
                <img class="verimg" src="https://via.placeholder.com/75"/>
                Follows the canon timeline.
       
       
       <br><br><br><br>
        </p>
            </ver>
            
            <ver>
                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Crossover  
    &emsp;&emsp;<b>Timeline:</b>    HxH
                </div><p>
                <a class="vertag" href="/tagged/VERSE TAG">verse tag</a>
                <img class="verimg" src="https://via.placeholder.com/75"/>
                Unknown to both himself and his adoptive parent, Dai originated from the Dark Continent and somehow washed up on shore of Dermline Island. After being found by the magical beasts there and raised, it becomes apparent once he's 12 years old that he's different. A special crest appears on the center of his forehead whenever Dai is angered, giving him the abilities of a Specialist for the time being, until its effects wear off. This power is a result of his mysterious Dark Continent origins.<p>

Dai is an Enhancer raised by the forest on Dermline Island and its magical beasts. Dermline Island is more or less uninhabitated, said to be infested with various monsters. Training relentlessly to become a hunter after hearing the tales his adoptive, beast, grandfather always told him. At the age of 12, he set out to take the exam and passed surprisingly before awakening his nen. Returning to his Island he was soon greeted by his soon-to-be tutor, Avan and educated on the works of Nen. While showing excellent skill and talent he struggles to for much of any power without the use of a weapon, therefore, swordplay is usually his combat style. In most cases, if angered enough, Dai unknowingly enhances said sword with overwhelming amounts of nen, making it cut down almost anything within its path.
       
       
       
       <br><br><br><br>
        </p>
            </ver>
            
            <ver>
                <div class="topbar">
                <b>Position:</b>    Crossover 
    &emsp;&emsp;<b>Timeline:</b>    BNHA
                </div><p>
                <a class="vertag" href="/tagged/VERSE TAG">verse tag</a>
                
                Dai is an aspiring Hero eager to hone his skills. In the beginninng, being adopted by his retired grandfather, Brass, after arriving on his doorstep mysteriously, the boy was raised and believed to be Quirkless. After having a run-in incident at the age of 12 where their little town was threatened by local thugs, Dai unexpectedly introduced his Quirk in attempt to fend off the thugs. It was later discovered that this Quirk responds to Dai's anger, giving him the strength of the elements. Prior to this, Dai's grandfather had taught him in hand to hand combat and swordplay when his dreams of becoming a Hero were slim to none. Now with new hopes and a hidden Quirk, Dai strives to become the Hero he always dreamed to be.<p>

                <b>Quirk:</b> 5th Element. This Quirk allows the user to use elemental attacks based on the 4 main elements (Earth, Air, Water, Fire) and even combine them, if the user is more experienced. However, the full extent and power of this can only be unleashed with the user's anger, otherwise the results are quite pitiful.<p>

                Years later, Dai is determined to apply to UA despite the limitations on his own Quirk and unfortunately with his inability to control it without his anger, he does not succeed and is enrolled in General Studies instead. His desires are yet again tested and nearly crushed until the Sports Festival, where he's truly able to display the power he possesses.
       
        </p>
            </ver>

                Apollo is sentenced to serve as mortal for a decade as punishment for angering Gaea. While his original sentence was set to be banished to Tartarus, his mother Leto convinced Zeus to reduce it to something less harsh. Therefore, Zeus decided to banish Apollo from Olympus for a decade instead. During this time, Apollo was to live his mortal life as Loxias, the Apprentice Herdsman. Admittedly, the God is quite displeased but makes the most of his mortal days nonetheless. He spends his days serving royalty as a herdsman's apprentice, often slacking off whenever opportune but doing as he's told nonetheless.<p>

In attempt to spare his boredom, Apollo sways his twin sister Artemis to visit him some nights in the midst of his mortality.

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ LOVE IS A POWERFUL THING. ❞</h2>

        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Eros is the greek god of Love, Friendship and Liberty. He is the oldest child of Ares and Aphrodite. He is often seen holding his infamous bow and arrow with tips in the shape of hearts. A wound with his arrow is enough to make man or god alike fall in love. Eros is a friendly young man, displaying surprising amounts of patience and kindness despite the nature of his parents. He is a loyal and devoted son and admires his mother, Aphrodite."<p>

"Eros has a sunny disposition but can sometimes unintentionally make rather ominous or eerie comments. The young God claims to have no hate in his heart and appears unfazed by most violent affairs but insists he has no issue doing favors for either of his parents."
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ BECAUSE MY PERSONALITY'S BAD! I WANNA GO BACK HOME AS A FIRST-CLASS SOURCERER AND MAKE EVERYONE CRY THEIR EYES OUT TO ME. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Maki is a tall athletic young woman with golden eyes and long black hair (dark green in the anime) normally tied into a ponytail. She has a fringe over her forehead with smaller strands framing her cheeks and is usually sporting a pair of glasses that allows her to see curses." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Maki_Zenin">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Maki is a very headstrong and straightforward person who tends to be quite blunt. She is strong willed and motivates herself to escape the ties of her sorcerer family. For her entire life, she has been mistreated and put down for being a woman and a non-sorcerer by the Zenins. Despite feeling cursed by her own family, Maki strives to become a sorcerer and prove everyone wrong, breaking the foundation of their way of life that she so rejects. Maki and Mai were originally going to stay together with the Zenin Family but the older twin decided she couldn't live that way. Rejected by her own family, Maki's bonds lie within her classmates whom she normally takes the leadership role with. She's very tough on them in training, very impatient and often hot-tempered. She only wishes to see them get stronger as they fight beside her and has taught many of her peers how to properly wield a variety of weapons, even if they had to get beaten up by her a lot to reach that point." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Maki_Zenin">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ CHEER UP GUYS, AT LEAST I'M HERE. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Nobara is a relatively short girl with a slim figure. She has mid-length orange hair that reaches to her neck that is styled with bangs that cover the left side of her forehead. Nobara has orange eyes, long eyelashes, and thin eyebrows of the same color." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Nobara_Kugisaki">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Maki is a very headstrong and straightforward person who tends to be quite blunt. She is strong willed and motivates herself to escape the ties of her sorcerer family. For her entire life, she has been mistreated and put down for being a woman and a non-sorcerer by the Zenins. Despite feeling cursed by her own family, Maki strives to become a sorcerer and prove everyone wrong, breaking the foundation of their way of life that she so rejects. Maki and Mai were originally going to stay together with the Zenin Family but the older twin decided she couldn't live that way. Rejected by her own family, Maki's bonds lie within her classmates whom she normally takes the leadership role with. She's very tough on them in training, very impatient and often hot-tempered. She only wishes to see them get stronger as they fight beside her and has taught many of her peers how to properly wield a variety of weapons, even if they had to get beaten up by her a lot to reach that point." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Nobara_Kugisaki">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ SO IT WAS ALL MY FAULT... ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Yuta is a young man of average height with disheveled black hair and dark blue eyes. His body language makes it easy to tell that Yuta is very stressed. His posture is very unconfident, and he has dark eyelids due to lack of sleep." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Yuta_Okkotsu">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Yuta was a very timid and lonely boy who was bullied a lot while growing up. Due to Rika haunting much of his early life, Yuta was unable to make connections with other people and has lost all confidence in himself. This makes it difficult for Yuta to interact with others, as they often scare him without meaning to or he's just too shy to speak to them. Even so, Yuta genuinely cared about other people and decided to isolate himself from them even if it means remaining alone. Maki Zenin called Yuta out for being a moody kid who's lived his entire life without goals. He acknowledged that this was true and used her advice to gain a resolve for being a Jujutsu Sorcerer. This helps Yuta realize that deep down he truly desires the confidence to feel like he belongs." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Yuta_Okkotsu">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>

            "Toge is a slim young man with light skin, brown eyes, and mid-length straight hair. He was born with the "Snake and Fangs" seal of the Inumaki family on his tongue and both cheeks, so his jujutsu student uniform with a high collar tailored into it that covers his mouth. While training, Toge wears a zipped-up dark collar underneath a white short sleeve shirt with athletic pants and shoes. After the Shibuya Incident, Toge lost his arm due to Sukuna's attack." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Toge_Inumaki">[Source]</a>

He doesn't speak in order to prevent accidentally cursing someone with his enchanted words." <a href="https://jujutsu-kaisen.fandom.com/wiki/Toge_Inumaki">[Source]</a>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ "THE OBEDIENT, LITTLE HELPLESS BLIND GIRL THAT YOU THINK I AM JUST ISN'T ME. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            Illegally good looking

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Toph Beifong is an earthbending master, one of the most powerful of her time, and the discoverer of metalbending. Blind since birth, Toph was constantly treated condescendingly because of her visual impairment, particularly by her overprotective parents, Lao and Poppy Beifong. Upon discovering badgermoles, earthbending animals who are also blind, she learned how to use earthbending as an extension of her senses. This gave her the ability to "see" every vibration that passes through the ground.<p>

Having developed her own unique style of earthbending, Toph acquired a toughened personality and became famous for winning underground earthbending tournaments under the alias "The Blind Bandit", doing so behind her parents' backs. Although initially uninterested in directly aiding the war effort, she eventually chose to leave behind her old life, and travel with Avatar Aang and his friends as his earthbending teacher, when her parents finally became unbearable for her.Toph's total mastery over earthbending, unique personality, and thoughtful pragmatism made her a valuable addition to the team." <a href="https://avatar.fandom.com/wiki/Toph_Beifong">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>

        <h4>About</h4>
        
        <table>

        <tr><th>Name:</th>      
            <td>    Hiei </td></tr>

        <tr><th>Birthday:</th>      
            <td>    ??? </td></tr>
            
        <tr><th>Gender:</th>      
            <td>    Male (he/him) </td></tr>

        <tr><th>Hobbies:</th>      
            <td>    Fighting, Committing various crimes </td></tr>

    <hr><h2 style="text-transform:lowercase;">❝ DON'T WORRY FOOL, WE'VE ENTERED INTO AN ALLIANCE AND I'M NOT THE TYPE TO BREAK IT. OF COURSE, AFTER WE WIN THE TOURNAMENT I CAN'T GUARANTEE ANYTHING. ❞</h2>
    
    <div class="dropdown">
        <p class="drop_title">  Appearance  ✧</p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            <!--insert images   →     <img src="IMG URL"/>    -->
            
            "Living up to his classic villainous persona, he usually dresses entirely in black. He wears a long black cloak-like jacket (with a white collar) and black pants tucked into black boots. In its initial appearance, he wears nothing beneath his cloak-like jacket and has a red tie at the center of his black pants but it was soon changes into two white belts where he frequently carries a sword with him that was strapped across his back. He later wears a black (and sometimes pale blue) sleeveless undershirt beneath the cloak-like jacket. He is the only one of the four main characters to never change his primary 'costume' during the series. The only exception was when he briefly wore light-colored Chinese battle costume at the start of the Dark Tournament." <a href="https://yuyuhakusho.fandom.com/wiki/Hiei">[Source]</a>

        </p></div><br>
        
        <p class="drop_title">✧  Personality   </p>
            <div class="drop_body">
            
            "Hiei prefers to keep his distance from others, so he often comes across as aloof and elusive. He has a rather cynical and even misanthropic view of the world around him, often belittling and mocking humans and their emotions and the significance they place on friendship and life. And while he is relatively taciturn, he occasionally squabbles with and insults his teammates, especially Kuwabara. It is obvious that deep down he holds a certain amount of respect and kinship for his teammates, but seems to be closest to Kurama and Yusuke. While he holds an affinity of kinship towards demons, this goes as equally far as his preference for humans, despising weaker demons, including braggarts and "tourists" who lack impetus for a degree of respect from him.<p>

As a fighter, Hiei is very unbiased when it comes to his enemies. He shows the same degree of ruthlessness to his foes - regardless of age or gender. This is seen when he terrorizes Ruka and the Masked-Fighter with threats of death as his power is returning. According to Kurama, however, he has an honor code that prevents him from going all out against an opponent he perceives as weaker than himself. In battle, Hiei has killed the most opponents on the team- often making good on a threat he made at the outset. He is also phenomenally arrogant, and has a tendency to underestimate his opponents; this was noted to be one of his greatest weak points." <a href="https://yuyuhakusho.fandom.com/wiki/Hiei">[Source]</a>
            
        </p></div><br>
    </div>
    
        </div>
    </swoop>

        *| CODING LIFEHACKS!
 
        insert a link:      <a href="URL">text</a>
        insert an image:    <img src="image URL"/>
        bold text:          <b> text </b> or <strong> text </strong>
        italics:            <i> text </i> or <em> text </em>
        underline:          <u> text </u> or <underline> text </underline>
        strike through:     <strike> text </strike>
        paragraphs:         <p> text text text </p>
        line breaks         <br>
        horizontal line:    <hr>
        headlines:          <h1>Headline 1</h1>
                            <h2>Headline 2</h2> <- default tumblr headline
                            <h3>Headline 3</h3>
                           
        LISTS
       
        numbered lists (circle)
       
            <ol>
            <li>Text</li>
            <li>Text</li>
            <li>Text</li>
            </ol>
       
        bullet point lists (stars)
       
            <ul>
            <li>Text</li>
            <li>Text</li>
            <li>Text</li>
            </ul>
